 mukhyamantri yogi adityanath ne adhikariyon se kaha he ki kanvad yatriyon par helicopter se phool or pankhudiyaan barasaane kaa bandobast kiya jaae
 All these instructions were issued at a meeting held at Lok Bhavan
 mukhyamantri ne saaf kar diya ki yatra ke dauraan deje band nahin honge lekin sirf bhajan bajaane kii hi ijaajat hogi, filmi gane katai nahin chalenge
 At the meeting, Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath asked the officials to identify the problems that may come in the way of the Kandar Yatra
 kanvad yatri bina kisi pareshaani apni sukhad yatra puri kar saken iske liye harek jone, jila or mandal str par vibhageeya baithken karne or aapas main talmail bithaane kaa aadesh diya gaya he
 Cleanliness is also to be taken care of during the journey
 mukhyamantri ne apane nirdeshon main spasht kar diya he ki tharmokol or plastic bag ke istemaal nahin kiye jaaenge
 Instructions have been given to ensure the safety of passengers
 mukhyamantri ne kaha ki prayagraj main abhi haal main beete kumbh mahotsav kii tarj par hi kanvad yatra kii taiyaari kii jaae
 All officials have been asked to identify Shiva temples in their area and ensure drinking water, sanitation, electricity and security there
 yogi adityanath ne baithak main adhikariyon se kaha ki kanvad yatra maarg par yaa jis jagah kanvad yatri thaharte hai, vahaan sharaab ke theke or avaidh boojadkhaane nahin chalane chahie
 This year, the last Somwari of Bakrid and Kavad Yatra is on 12 August on the same day
 mukhyamantri yogi adityanath ne adhikariyon ko nirdesh diya he ki us din pashuon ke avaidh vadh kii ijaajat nahin hogi
 Finland company HMD Global will launch three Nokia smartphones in India today
 sabase pehle inhen mobile world congress ke dauraan launch kiya gaya tha
 Although the company has already launched Nokia 3310 in India, but these three smartphones are very important in the Indian market
 kyonki yahi teen smartphone duniya ke sabase bade smartphone bazaar main nokia ko phir uski badshahath kaayam karne main madad kar sakate hai
 These are three Android smartphones - Nokia 3, Nokia 5 and Nokia 6
 aaj in teenon smartphone kii keemten, uplabdhta or ophers ke bare main elaan hoga
 According to reports, Nokia 3 will cost around 9 thousand rupees
 jabaki Nokia 6 or Nokia 5 kii keemat kramshah 15 hajaar rupee or 11 hajaar rupee hone kii ummid he
 However, these smartphones will be officially launched in India in a few hours from now and during this time we will also tell you about its prices
 itnaa hi nahin, launch hone ke baad ham aapako yah bhi bataaenge ki kya is price segment main isse behatar opshan aapke paas maujuud hai
 Nokia 5 Specifications New NOKIA 5 in 5
 2 inch kaa phul HD disple he jo gorilla glass ke saath aayega

 NOKIA 5 main 16GB kaa internal storage diya gaya he jise card kii sahaayta se 128GB tak badhaayaa ja saktaa he
 Nokia 6 specification Nokia 6 with Gorilla Glass
 5 inch kaphul echdi disple he
 This device has 4GB RAM and 64GB internal memory with Snapdragon 430 Soc processor
 dual sim vaale Nokia 6 main fast charging saport ke saath 3000mah kaa non-removable bydaree di gai he
 Nokia 3 specification has 16GB internal memory with 2GB of RAM
 yah ek mid range smartphone he jisaki bild quality kaaphi behatar he
 It has an MTK quadcore processor
 iskaa back aluminium or policarbonate kaa bana he jo ise premium tach detaa he
 In Uttar Pradesh's Yogi Adityanath government, Cabinet Minister Omprakash Rajbhar himself is not talking about breaking away from the alliance, but it seems that he wants the BJP to separate him from the alliance
 isiilie aaj varanasi main unhone kaha ki main aisi harakat karata hum ki bijepi mujhe nikaal de
 However, when asked how long his love for the BJP will last, he said that until the BJP expels him
 upi sarkaar main rahete hue apane bagawati sur ke liye pahachaane jane vaale cabinet mantri omprakash rajbhar kaa bijepi se chal rahaa shityudh ab apane charam par aa pahunchaa he
 As a result of this, on Saturday, Omprakash Rajbhar made it clear that the BJP will expel him from the alliance
 aisa isliye hoga kyonki ve kehete hai ki main sadaken banavaane kii baat karata hum
 Talk about housing, pension, toilets, education and medicine, to make three categories among backward
 aarakshan mil rahaa he, lekin laabh nahin
 i am angry for this unhone saaf chetavanee bhi de di ki uttar pradesh main pichhadi jati ke aarakshan main vibhaajan nahin hua to bahut bura parinaam hoga
 He said that the heat has increased a lot, and a big storm will come after 26 June
 omprakash rajbhar ne shanivaar dopaher apane gaanv main fawda uthaa kar khud hi road banaate video bhi post kiya tha or tasviren bhi post kii
 He is angry that he is not being heard in the BJP government and his request to build a 500-meter road in the village at the wedding of the son was not heard
 sadak banane ke liye khud uthaaya fawdarajbhar ne sadak banane ke liye khud fawda uthaaya or yogi sarkaar par nishaanaa sadhate hue kaha ki jab ek mantri ke ghar sadak nahin ban sakati to janata bhagwaan bharose he
 Actually on June 24, Omprakash Rajbhar's son is married
 lekin gaanv main sadak nahin ban pai he
 Despite constantly urging his government to build a village road, when the road was not built, the minister, his family and the people of the village started picking up the shovel themselves and building the road
 mantri ke chote bete ne media ko bayaan jari kar kaha ki 500 meter sadak banane ke liye lagbhag 6 maah pehle prastaav diya tha
 On June 24, Minister Omprakash Rajbhar's elder son Arvind is married, but the work could not be done
 bataa den ki mantri omprakash rajbhar ke ghar varanasi ke sindhaura gaanv main shaadi samaaroh or bhoj he
 In which vips, Cabinet Ministers, Ministers of State, mps and mlas are expected to come
 jab sarkaar sadak nahin bana pai to khud mantri omprakash rajbhar apane donon beton aravid rajbhar, arun rajbhar ne saath fawda uthaakar sadak banane kii koshish main jute gaye
 There have been reports of electoral violence during voting in Haryana assembly elections
 kahin goli to kahin tod-phod marpet to kahin jhadap or jor-aazamaaish kii khabaren aa rahi hai
 There have been clashes between the BJP and the INLD from Sirsa to Hisar
 sirsa main bijepi or ieneldi ke bich jhadap kii khabar he
 Meanwhile, there have also been reports of firing, in which an INLD worker has been injured
 sirsa main hi haryana lokhit party ke ummidavaar gopal kanda or ieneldi kaaryakartaaon ke bich marpet or jhadap kii khabar he
 Kanda is reported to have slapped the brother of INLD candidate Butter Singla, following which the dispute between the two leaders escalated
 isi dauraan ieneldi kaaryakarta bhi uttejit ho uthe or unhone gopal kanda kii gaadi ko tod diya
 Apart from this, BJP and INLD clashed in Narnaund, Hisar
 uttar pradesh main svachh bharat mishan kii raftaar kaaphi tej ho gai he
 The Akhilesh government has demanded the funds again from the central government by spending the amount given by the central government ahead of time
 mishan se jude adhikariyon ke anusaar, khule main shouch (odief) ko rokane ke liye jilon main abhiyaan kaaphi teji se chalaaya ja rahaa he or logon par iskaa kaaphi sakaaratmak prabhaav pad rahaa he
 Amit Gupta, Special Secretary to Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav and Director of Swachh Bharat Mission in Uttar Pradesh, gave this information during a special conversation with IANS
 unhone pradesh main svachh bharat mishan ko lekar chalaae ja rahe abhiyaan par vistaar se jaankaree di
 Amit Gupta said that this is happening for the first time when the funds received from the central government have been spent before time
 sarkaar ne doguni dhanrashi dene kii maang kii he
 Although the funds released by the Center were delayed a lot, but despite this there was no impact on the campaign
 gupta ne bataaya ki svachh bharat mishan ke tahat centre sarkaar kaa hissaa 60 pratishat hota he or 40 pratishat bajet rajya sarkaar vahan karti he
 The portion (about Rs 600 crore) released by the central government has been spent completely
 ab centre sarkaar se doguni dhanrashi maangi gai he
 However, Amit Gupta appeared quite confident about the campaign being run for the Clean India Mission in the state
 unhone bataaya ki is abhiyaan ko lekar khud mukhyamantri kaaphi gambhir hai or samay-samay par isaki jaankaree lete rahete hai
 The Special Secretary to the Chief Minister informed that under the scheme, about 40 crore rupees are released to each district
 isi dhanrashi se yah abhiyaan chalaaya jaataa he
 Till now it has been very successful
 shuruyaat main keval ek jila hi odief se mukt ho paaya tha, lekin ab teen jile khule main shouch se mukt ho gaye hai
 He informed that the entire amount has been spent under the Swachh Bharat Abhiyan in Bijnor, Shamli and Kannauj districts as well
 yahaan bhi kaaphi teji se is abhiyaan ko chalaaya ja rahaa he, jin jilon main acha kaam ho rahaa he vahaan zyada paisa bhi diya jaataa he
 According to Amit Gupta, the help of many voluntary organizations is also taken to make people aware against open defecation
 unki madad se gramin ilaakon main isko lekar logon ko jaagruk kiya jaataa he
 From time to time, attempts are made to convince people through street plays
 amit gupta ne bataaya ki is baat kaa bhi dhyaan rakhaa gaya he ki jo bhi gaanv puri tarah khule main shouch se mukt ho chuke hai, vahaan likhe gaye slogan evam waal painting se bhi pradarshit hona chahie ki yah gaanv khule main shouch karne kii pratha se mukt ho chuke hai
 The IAS officer said that Swachh Bharat Mission (gramin) is an important program run by the Government of India, which aims to free India from the curse of impurity
 unhone kaha, "khule main shouch kii pravriti desh or raashtra ke liye abhishaap he, jo vishwa main desh ke gaurav ko dhoomil kar rahi he
 In addition, thousands of children die every day from this dirty and shameful practice and suffer from serious diseases
 " The IAS officer said that every day women are forced to suffer the pain and shame of defecating in the open
 isi kupratha ke chalate mahila ke prati aparaadh bhi utpann hote hai, jo kabhi-kabhi vikaraal rup dhaaran karte hue kanoon vyavastha ke liye chunauti ban jate hai
 Amit Gupta said, "we have to end the curse of the practice of open defecation in order to save the lives of our communities, their healthy future and respect for the female world and protect our community, and this is only possible
" When the true perception of this curse arises in our mind
 " The Director of the Swachh Bharat Mission has also given strict warning to the District Magistrates of many districts due to negligence in this campaign
 tippaniyan According to sources, the Swachh Bharat Mission is a big mission in itself, but still many district magistrates are being subjected to this
 kai jiladhikari aise bhi hai, jo sarkaar dwaara shauchalay nirmaan ke paise tak ko dabaae baithe hai, jisko lekar nideshak ne sakht rukh apanaaya he

 He gave detailed information on the campaign being run for the Swachh Bharat Mission in the state
 amit gupta ne kaha ki aisa pehali baar ho rahaa he jab centre sarkaar kii ore se mili dhanrashi samay se pehle hi kharch ho gai he
 The government has demanded double the amount
 haalanki, centre ne pehle jo dhanrashi jari kii usamen kaaphi deree hui, lekin iske baavjood is abhiyaan par uskaa koi asar nahin padaa
 Gupta said that under the Swachh Bharat Mission, the central government's share is 60 percent and the state government bears 40 percent of the budget
 centre sarkaar ne jo hissaa (lagbhag 600 karod rupee) jari kiya tha, vah puraa kharch ho chukaa he
